Local Open Scope cat.

Section Inserters.
  Context {B : bicat}
          {b₁ b₂ : B}
          {f g : b₁ --> b₂}.

  (**
   1. Cones
   *)
  Definition inserter_cone
    : UU
    := ∑ (i : B)
         (m : i --> b₁),
       m · f ==> m · g.

  Definition make_inserter_cone
             (i : B)
             (m : i --> b₁)
             (α : m · f ==> m · g)
    : inserter_cone
    := i ,, m ,, α.

  Coercion inserter_cone_ob
           (cone : inserter_cone)
    : B
    := pr1 cone.

  Definition inserter_cone_pr1
             (cone : inserter_cone)
    : cone --> b₁
    := pr12 cone.

  Definition inserter_cone_cell
             (cone : inserter_cone)
    : inserter_cone_pr1 cone · f ==> inserter_cone_pr1 cone · g
    := pr22 cone.

  Definition inserter_1cell
             (cone₁ cone₂ : inserter_cone)
    : UU
    := ∑ (k : cone₁ --> cone₂)
         (α : invertible_2cell
                (k · inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂)
                (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₁)),
       (k ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone₂)
       • lassociator _ _ _
       • (α ▹ g)
       =
       lassociator _ _ _
       • (α ▹ f)
       • inserter_cone_cell cone₁.

  Definition make_inserter_1cell
             {cone₁ cone₂ : inserter_cone}
             (k : cone₁ --> cone₂)
             (α : invertible_2cell
                    (k · inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂)
                    (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₁))
             (p : (k ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone₂)
                  • lassociator _ _ _
                  • (α ▹ g)
                  =
                  lassociator _ _ _
                  • (α ▹ f)
                  • inserter_cone_cell cone₁)
    : inserter_1cell cone₁ cone₂
    := k ,, α ,, p.

  Coercion inserter_1cell_mor
           {cone₁ cone₂ : inserter_cone}
           (u : inserter_1cell cone₁ cone₂)
    : cone₁ --> cone₂
    := pr1 u.

  Definition inserter_1cell_pr1
             {cone₁ cone₂ : inserter_cone}
             (u : inserter_1cell cone₁ cone₂)
    : invertible_2cell
        (u · inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂)
        (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₁)
    := pr12 u.

  Definition inserter_1cell_cell
             {cone₁ cone₂ : inserter_cone}
             (u : inserter_1cell cone₁ cone₂)
    : (_ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone₂)
       • lassociator _ _ _
       • (inserter_1cell_pr1 u ▹ g)
       =
       lassociator _ _ _
       • (inserter_1cell_pr1 u ▹ f)
       • inserter_cone_cell cone₁
    := pr22 u.

  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
cone₁, cone₂: inserter_cone
φ, ψ: inserter_1cell cone₁ cone₂
p₁: pr1 φ = pr1 ψ
p₂: pr112 φ =
(idtoiso_2_1 (pr1 φ) (pr1 ψ) p₁
 ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) • pr112 ψ
φ = ψ

  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
cone₁, cone₂: inserter_cone
φ, ψ: inserter_1cell cone₁ cone₂
p₁: pr1 φ = pr1 ψ
p₂: pr112 φ =
(idtoiso_2_1 (pr1 φ) (pr1 ψ) p₁
 ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) • pr112 ψ
φ = ψ

    
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
cone₁, cone₂: inserter_cone
φ₁: B ⟦ cone₁, cone₂ ⟧
φ₂: invertible_2cell (φ₁ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂)
  (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₁)
φ₃: ((φ₁ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone₂)
 • lassociator φ₁ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) g)
• (φ₂ ▹ g) =
(lassociator φ₁ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) f
 • (φ₂ ▹ f)) • inserter_cone_cell cone₁
ψ: inserter_1cell cone₁ cone₂
p₁: pr1 (φ₁,, φ₂,, φ₃) = pr1 ψ
p₂: pr112 (φ₁,, φ₂,, φ₃) =
(idtoiso_2_1 (pr1 (φ₁,, φ₂,, φ₃)) (pr1 ψ) p₁
 ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) • pr112 ψ
φ₁,, φ₂,, φ₃ = ψ

    
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
cone₁, cone₂: inserter_cone
φ₁: B ⟦ cone₁, cone₂ ⟧
φ₂: invertible_2cell (φ₁ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂)
  (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₁)
φ₃: ((φ₁ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone₂)
 • lassociator φ₁ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) g)
• (φ₂ ▹ g) =
(lassociator φ₁ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) f
 • (φ₂ ▹ f)) • inserter_cone_cell cone₁
ψ₁: B ⟦ cone₁, cone₂ ⟧
ψ₂: invertible_2cell (ψ₁ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂)
  (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₁)
ψ₃: ((ψ₁ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone₂)
 • lassociator ψ₁ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) g)
• (ψ₂ ▹ g) =
(lassociator ψ₁ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) f
 • (ψ₂ ▹ f)) • inserter_cone_cell cone₁
p₁: pr1 (φ₁,, φ₂,, φ₃) = pr1 (ψ₁,, ψ₂,, ψ₃)
p₂: pr112 (φ₁,, φ₂,, φ₃) =
(idtoiso_2_1 (pr1 (φ₁,, φ₂,, φ₃))
   (pr1 (ψ₁,, ψ₂,, ψ₃)) p₁
 ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂)
• pr112 (ψ₁,, ψ₂,, ψ₃)
φ₁,, φ₂,, φ₃ = ψ₁,, ψ₂,, ψ₃

    
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
cone₁, cone₂: inserter_cone
φ₁: B ⟦ cone₁, cone₂ ⟧
φ₂: invertible_2cell (φ₁ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂)
  (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₁)

  (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₁)
ψ₃: ((ψ₁ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone₂)
 • lassociator ψ₁ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) g)
• (ψ₂ ▹ g) =
(lassociator ψ₁ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) f
 • (ψ₂ ▹ f)) • inserter_cone_cell cone₁
p₁: φ₁ = ψ₁
p₂: pr1 φ₂ =
(idtoiso_2_1 φ₁ ψ₁ p₁ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂)
• pr1 ψ₂
φ₁,, φ₂,, φ₃ = ψ₁,, ψ₂,, ψ₃

    • (x ▹ f)) • inserter_cone_cell cone₁)

B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
cone₁, cone₂: inserter_cone
φ₁: B ⟦ cone₁, cone₂ ⟧
φ₂: invertible_2cell (φ₁ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂)
  (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₁)
φ₃: ((φ₁ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone₂)
 • lassociator φ₁ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) g)
• (φ₂ ▹ g) =
(lassociator φ₁ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) f
 • (φ₂ ▹ f)) • inserter_cone_cell cone₁
ψ₂: invertible_2cell (φ₁ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂)
  (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₁)
ψ₃: ((φ₁ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone₂)
 • lassociator φ₁ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) g)
• (ψ₂ ▹ g) =
(lassociator φ₁ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) f
 • (ψ₂ ▹ f)) • inserter_cone_cell cone₁
p₂: pr1 φ₂ =
(idtoiso_2_1 φ₁ φ₁ (idpath φ₁)
 ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone₂) • 
pr1 ψ₂
isPredicate is_invertible_2cell

 • (φ₂ ▹ f)) • inserter_cone_cell cone₁

  (inserter_cone_pr1 cone₁)

pr1 ψ₂

inserter_cone_pr1 cone₁
isaprop (is_invertible_2cell x)

  (**
   2. The universal mapping property
   *)
  Section UniversalMappingProperty.
    Context (cone : inserter_cone).

    Definition has_inserter_ump_1
      : UU
      := ∏ (other_cone : inserter_cone),
         inserter_1cell other_cone cone.

    Definition has_inserter_ump_2
      : UU
      := ∏ (x : B)
           (u₁ u₂ : x --> cone)
           (α : u₁ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone
                ==>
                u₂ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone)
           (p : rassociator _ _ _
                • (u₁ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone)
                • lassociator _ _ _
                • (α ▹ g)
                =
                (α ▹ f)
                • rassociator _ _ _
                • (u₂ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone)
                • lassociator _ _ _),
         ∑ (ζ : u₁ ==> u₂),
         ζ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone = α.

    Definition has_inserter_ump_eq
      : UU
      := ∏ (x : B)
           (u₁ u₂ : x --> cone)
           (α : u₁ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone
                ==>
                u₂ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone)
           (p : rassociator _ _ _
                • (u₁ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone)
                • lassociator _ _ _
                • (α ▹ g)
                =
                (α ▹ f)
                • rassociator _ _ _
                • (u₂ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone)
                • lassociator _ _ _)
           (φ₁ φ₂ : u₁ ==> u₂)
           (q₁ : φ₁ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone = α)
           (q₂ : φ₂ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone = α),
         φ₁ = φ₂.

    Definition has_inserter_ump
      : UU
      := has_inserter_ump_1 × has_inserter_ump_2 × has_inserter_ump_eq.
  End UniversalMappingProperty.

  Section Projections.
    Context {cone : inserter_cone}
            (H : has_inserter_ump cone).

    Definition inserter_ump_mor
               {i : B}
               (m : i --> b₁)
               (α : m · f ==> m · g)
      : i --> cone
      := pr1 H (make_inserter_cone i m α).

    Definition inserter_ump_mor_pr1
               {i : B}
               (m : i --> b₁)
               (α : m · f ==> m · g)
      : invertible_2cell
          (inserter_ump_mor m α · inserter_cone_pr1 cone)
          m
      := inserter_1cell_pr1 (pr1 H (make_inserter_cone i m α)).

    Definition inserter_ump_mor_cell
               {i : B}
               (m : i --> b₁)
               (α : m · f ==> m · g)
      : (_ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone)
        • lassociator _ _ _
        • (inserter_ump_mor_pr1 m α ▹ g)
        =
        lassociator _ _ _
        • (inserter_ump_mor_pr1 m α ▹ f)
        • α
      := inserter_1cell_cell (pr1 H (make_inserter_cone i m α)).

    Definition inserter_ump_cell
               {x : B}
               {u₁ u₂ : x --> cone}
               (α : u₁ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone
                    ==>
                    u₂ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone)
               (p : rassociator _ _ _
                    • (u₁ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone)
                    • lassociator _ _ _
                    • (α ▹ g)
                    =
                    (α ▹ f)
                    • rassociator _ _ _
                    • (u₂ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone)
                    • lassociator _ _ _)
      : u₁ ==> u₂
      := pr1 (pr12 H x u₁ u₂ α p).

    Definition inserter_ump_cell_pr1
               {x : B}
               {u₁ u₂ : x --> cone}
               (α : u₁ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone
                    ==>
                    u₂ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone)
               (p : rassociator _ _ _
                    • (u₁ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone)
                    • lassociator _ _ _
                    • (α ▹ g)
                    =
                    (α ▹ f)
                    • rassociator _ _ _
                    • (u₂ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone)
                    • lassociator _ _ _)
      : inserter_ump_cell α p ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone = α
      := pr2 (pr12 H x u₁ u₂ α p).

    Definition inserter_ump_eq
               {x : B}
               {u₁ u₂ : x --> cone}
               (α : u₁ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone
                    ==>
                    u₂ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone)
               (p : rassociator _ _ _
                    • (u₁ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone)
                    • lassociator _ _ _
                    • (α ▹ g)
                    =
                    (α ▹ f)
                    • rassociator _ _ _
                    • (u₂ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone)
                    • lassociator _ _ _)
               (φ₁ φ₂ : u₁ ==> u₂)
               (q₁ : φ₁ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone = α)
               (q₂ : φ₂ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone = α)
      : φ₁ = φ₂
      := pr22 H x u₁ u₂ α p φ₁ φ₂ q₁ q₂.

φ₁, φ₂: u₁ ==> u₂
p: ((rassociator u₁ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f
  • (u₁ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone))

• ((φ₁ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone) ▹ g) =
((((φ₁ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone) ▹ f)
  • rassociator u₂ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f)
 • (u₂ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone))
• lassociator u₂ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g
q: φ₁ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone =
φ₂ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone
φ₁ = φ₂

b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧

  • (u₁ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone))
 • lassociator u₁ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g)
• ((φ₁ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone) ▹ g) =
((((φ₁ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone) ▹ f)
  • rassociator u₂ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f)
 • (u₂ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone))
• lassociator u₂ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g
q: φ₁ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone =
φ₂ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone

φ₁ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone

  End Projections.

  Section Invertible2CellInserterUMP.
    Context {cone : inserter_cone}
            (H : has_inserter_ump cone)
            {x : B}
            {u₁ u₂ : x --> cone}
            (α : u₁ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone
                 ==>
                 u₂ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone)
            (p : rassociator _ _ _
                 • (u₁ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone)
                 • lassociator _ _ _
                 • (α ▹ g)
                 =
                 (α ▹ f)
                 • rassociator _ _ _
                 • (u₂ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone)
                 • lassociator _ _ _)
            (Hα : is_invertible_2cell α).

    
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
cone: inserter_cone
H: has_inserter_ump cone
x: B
u₁, u₂: B ⟦ x, cone ⟧
α: u₁ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone ==>
u₂ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone
p: ((rassociator u₁ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f
  • (u₁ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone))
 • lassociator u₁ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g)
• (α ▹ g) =
(((α ▹ f)
  • rassociator u₂ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f)
 • (u₂ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone))
• lassociator u₂ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g
Hα: is_invertible_2cell α

   • (lassociator u₁ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g
      • ((α ▹ g) • (Hα ^-1 ▹ g)))) =
((α • Hα ^-1) ▹ f)
• (rassociator u₁ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f
   • ((u₁ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone)
      • lassociator u₁ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g))

                            ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone)
                           • lassociator
                               (pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q))
                               (inserter_cone_pr1 cone)
                               g)))
                    (vassocl
                       (((inserter_1cell_pr1
                            (pr1 χ₁ q) ▹ f)

                               (pr1 χ₂ q)) ^-1 ▹ f))
                        • rassociator (pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q))
                            (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f)
                       (pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q)
                        ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone)
                       (lassociator (pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q))
                          (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g)))
                 (vassocl
                    (rassociator (pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q))
                       (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f)
                    (pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q)
                     ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone)
                    (lassociator (pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q))
                       (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g
                     • ((inserter_1cell_pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q)
                         ▹ g)
                        • ((inserter_1cell_pr1
                              (pr1 χ₂ q)) ^-1 ▹ g)))))
              (vassocl
                 (rassociator (pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q))
                    (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f
                  • (pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q)
                     ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone))
                 (lassociator (pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q))
                    (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g)
                 ((inserter_1cell_pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q) ▹ g)
                  • ((inserter_1cell_pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q))
                     ^-1 ▹ g))))
           ((inserter_1cell_pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q)
             • (inserter_1cell_pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q)) ^-1)
            ▹ f)
           (rwhisker_vcomp f
              (inserter_1cell_pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q))
              (inserter_1cell_pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q)) ^-1))
        ((inserter_1cell_pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q)
          • (inserter_1cell_pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q)) ^-1) ▹ g)
        (rwhisker_vcomp g
           (inserter_1cell_pr1 (pr1 χ₁ q))
           (inserter_1cell_pr1 (pr1 χ₂ q)) ^-1)))

B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧

h: dialgebra (post_comp x f) (post_comp x g)
is_z_isomorphism
  (pr1
     (((let X :=
          λ (H : has_inserter_ump cone) (i : B)
          (m : B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧) (α : m · f ==> m · g),
          pr1 (inserter_ump_mor_pr1 H m α) in
        X H x (pr1 h) (pr2 h))
       :
       hom x b₁
       ⟦ pr1
           (inserter_cone_functor cone x
              (inserter_ump_mor H (pr1 h) (pr2 h))),
       pr1 h ⟧),,
      (make_is_universal_inserter_cone_essentially_surjective_subproof
         h
       :
       (λ f0 : hom x b₁
               ⟦ pr1
                   (inserter_cone_functor cone x
                      (inserter_ump_mor H (pr1 h)
                         (pr2 h))), pr1 h ⟧,
        Core.mor_disp
          (pr2
             (inserter_cone_functor cone x
                (inserter_ump_mor H (pr1 h) (pr2 h))))
          (pr2 h) f0)
         ((let X :=
             λ (H : has_inserter_ump cone) (i : B)
             (m : B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧) (α : m · f ==> m · g),
             pr1 (inserter_ump_mor_pr1 H m α) in
           X H x (pr1 h) (pr2 h))
          :
          hom x b₁
          ⟦ pr1
              (inserter_cone_functor cone x
                 (inserter_ump_mor H (pr1 h) (pr2 h))),
          pr1 h ⟧))))

          ⟦ pr1
              (inserter_cone_functor cone x
                 (inserter_ump_mor H (pr1 h) (pr2 h))),
          pr1 h ⟧))))

          apply property_from_invertible_2cell.
    Defined.
  End MakeUniversalInserterCone.

        : q --> cone
        := right_adjoint (H q) alg.

       • (u₂ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone))
      • lassociator u₂ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g))

        apply cellset_property.
      
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
cone: inserter_cone
H: is_universal_inserter_cone cone
x: B
u₁, u₂: B ⟦ x, cone ⟧
α: u₁ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone ==>
u₂ · inserter_cone_pr1 cone
p: ((rassociator u₁ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f
  • (u₁ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone))
 • lassociator u₁ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g)
• (α ▹ g) =
(((α ▹ f)
  • rassociator u₂ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f)
 • (u₂ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone))
• lassociator u₂ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g
φ₁, φ₂: u₁ ==> u₂
q₁: φ₁ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone = α
q₂: φ₂ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone = α
pr1
  ((φ₁ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone),,
   inserter_cone_functor_data_subproof cone x u₁ u₂ φ₁) =
pr1
  ((φ₂ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone),,
   inserter_cone_functor_data_subproof cone x u₁ u₂ φ₂)

  • (u₁ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone))

  • rassociator u₂ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) f)
 • (u₂ ◃ inserter_cone_cell cone))
• lassociator u₂ (inserter_cone_pr1 cone) g
φ₁, φ₂: u₁ ==> u₂
q₁: φ₁ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone = α

φ₁ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone =
φ₂ ▹ inserter_cone_pr1 cone

      exact (q₁ @ !q₂).
    Qed.

Arguments inserter_cone {_ _ _} _ _.

(**
 4. Bicategories with inserters
 *)
Definition has_inserters
           (B : bicat)
  : UU
  := ∏ (b₁ b₂ : B)
       (f g : b₁ --> b₂),
     ∑ (i : B)
       (m : i --> b₁)
       (α : m · f ==> m · g),
     has_inserter_ump (make_inserter_cone i m α).

(**
 5. Inserters are faithful
 *)

B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: m · f ==> m · g
H: has_inserter_ump (make_inserter_cone i m α)
faithful_1cell m


B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: m · f ==> m · g
H: has_inserter_ump (make_inserter_cone i m α)
faithful_1cell m

  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: m · f ==> m · g
H: has_inserter_ump (make_inserter_cone i m α)
x: B
g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β₁, β₂: g₁ ==> g₂
p: β₁ ▹ m = β₂ ▹ m
β₁ = β₂

  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: m · f ==> m · g
H: has_inserter_ump (make_inserter_cone i m α)
x: B

β₁, β₂: g₁ ==> g₂
p: β₁ ▹ m = β₂ ▹ m
((rassociator g₁ m f • (g₁ ◃ α)) • lassociator g₁ m g)
• ((β₁ ▹ m) ▹ g) =
((((β₁ ▹ m) ▹ f) • rassociator g₂ m f) • (g₂ ◃ α))
• lassociator g₂ m g
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B

b₁, b₂: B

• ((β₁ ▹ m) ▹ g) =
((((β₁ ▹ m) ▹ f) • rassociator g₂ m f) • (g₂ ◃ α))
• lassociator g₂ m g
 abstract
      (rewrite rwhisker_rwhisker_alt ;
       rewrite !vassocl ;
       apply maponpaths ;
       rewrite rwhisker_rwhisker ;
       rewrite !vassocr ;
       apply maponpaths_2 ;
       refine (!_) ;
       apply vcomp_whisker).

p: β₁ ▹ m = β₂ ▹ m
β₁ ▹ m = β₂ ▹ m
 exact p.
Defined.

(**
 6. Inserters are conservative
 *)
Section InserterConservative.
  Context {B : bicat}
          {b₁ b₂ : B}
          {f g : b₁ --> b₂}
          {i : B}
          (m : i --> b₁)
          (α : m · f ==> m · g)
          (H : has_inserter_ump (make_inserter_cone i m α))
          {x : B}
          {g₁ g₂ : x --> i}
          (β : g₁ ==> g₂)
          (Hβ : is_invertible_2cell (β ▹ m)).

  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: m · f ==> m · g
H: has_inserter_ump (make_inserter_cone i m α)
x: B
g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β: g₁ ==> g₂
Hβ: is_invertible_2cell (β ▹ m)
g₂ ==> g₁

  
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: m · f ==> m · g
H: has_inserter_ump (make_inserter_cone i m α)
x: B
g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β: g₁ ==> g₂
Hβ: is_invertible_2cell (β ▹ m)
g₂ ==> g₁

    
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: m · f ==> m · g
H: has_inserter_ump (make_inserter_cone i m α)
x: B
g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β: g₁ ==> g₂
Hβ: is_invertible_2cell (β ▹ m)
g₂ · inserter_cone_pr1 (make_inserter_cone i m α) ==>
g₁ · inserter_cone_pr1 (make_inserter_cone i m α)
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: m · f ==> m · g
H: has_inserter_ump (make_inserter_cone i m α)
x: B
g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β: g₁ ==> g₂
Hβ: is_invertible_2cell (β ▹ m)
((rassociator g₂
    (inserter_cone_pr1 (make_inserter_cone i m α)) f
  • (g₂
     ◃ inserter_cone_cell (make_inserter_cone i m α)))
 • lassociator g₂
     (inserter_cone_pr1 (make_inserter_cone i m α)) g)
• (?α ▹ g) =
(((?α ▹ f)
  • rassociator g₁
      (inserter_cone_pr1 (make_inserter_cone i m α)) f)
 • (g₁ ◃ inserter_cone_cell (make_inserter_cone i m α)))
• lassociator g₁
    (inserter_cone_pr1 (make_inserter_cone i m α)) g

    
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: m · f ==> m · g
H: has_inserter_ump (make_inserter_cone i m α)
x: B
g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β: g₁ ==> g₂
Hβ: is_invertible_2cell (β ▹ m)
g₂ · inserter_cone_pr1 (make_inserter_cone i m α) ==>
g₁ · inserter_cone_pr1 (make_inserter_cone i m α)
 exact Hβ^-1.
    
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: m · f ==> m · g

Hβ: is_invertible_2cell (β ▹ m)
((rassociator g₂
    (inserter_cone_pr1 (make_inserter_cone i m α)) f
  • (g₂
     ◃ inserter_cone_cell (make_inserter_cone i m α)))
 • lassociator g₂
     (inserter_cone_pr1 (make_inserter_cone i m α)) g)
• (Hβ ^-1 ▹ g) =
(((Hβ ^-1 ▹ f)
  • rassociator g₁
      (inserter_cone_pr1 (make_inserter_cone i m α)) f)
 • (g₁ ◃ inserter_cone_cell (make_inserter_cone i m α)))
• lassociator g₁
    (inserter_cone_pr1 (make_inserter_cone i m α)) g
 abstract
        (cbn ;
         use vcomp_move_R_Mp ; [ is_iso | ] ; cbn ;
         rewrite !vassocl ;
         rewrite rwhisker_rwhisker ;
         use vcomp_move_L_pM ; [ is_iso | ] ; cbn ;
         rewrite !vassocr ;
         apply maponpaths_2 ;
         rewrite rwhisker_rwhisker_alt ;
         rewrite !vassocl ;
         apply maponpaths ;
         rewrite vcomp_whisker ;
         apply idpath).
  Defined.

   • (((β • inserter_conservative_inv) ▹ m) ▹ g)) =

i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: m · f ==> m · g
H: has_inserter_ump (make_inserter_cone i m α)
x: B
g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β: g₁ ==> g₂
Hβ: is_invertible_2cell (β ▹ m)
(g₁ ◃ α) • ((β • inserter_conservative_inv) ▹ m · g) =
((β • inserter_conservative_inv) ▹ m · f) • (g₁ ◃ α)

      
B: bicat
b₁, b₂: B
f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: m · f ==> m · g
H: has_inserter_ump (make_inserter_cone i m α)
x: B
g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β: g₁ ==> g₂
Hβ: is_invertible_2cell (β ▹ m)
(g₁ ◃ α) • ((β • inserter_conservative_inv) ▹ m · g) =
(g₁ ◃ α) • ((β • inserter_conservative_inv) ▹ m · g)

      apply idpath.
    
B: bicat

(β • inserter_conservative_inv) ▹ m = id₂ g₁ ▹ m

(β ▹ m)

     inserter_conservative_inv_subproof ▹ m) =

      apply vcomp_rinv.
  Qed.

B: bicat

f, g: B ⟦ b₁, b₂ ⟧
i: B
m: B ⟦ i, b₁ ⟧
α: m · f ==> m · g
H: has_inserter_ump (make_inserter_cone i m α)

g₁, g₂: B ⟦ x, i ⟧
β: g₁ ==> g₂
Hβ: is_invertible_2cell (β ▹ m)
((rassociator g₂ m f • (g₂ ◃ α)) • lassociator g₂ m g)
• (((inserter_conservative_inv • β) ▹ m) ▹ g) =
(((((inserter_conservative_inv • β) ▹ m) ▹ f)
  • rassociator g₂ m f) • (g₂ ◃ α))
• lassociator g₂ m g

   • ((g₂ ◃ α) • lassociator g₂ m g))

End InserterConservative.

Defined.
